add_namespace = germany
add_namespace = proxy
#DEFENDER 20 Europe
country_event = {
	id = germany.1
	title = germany.1.t
	desc = germany.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_defender_20
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	minor_flavor = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.1 immediate"
			army_experience = 25
			navy_experience = 25
			air_experience = 25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.1.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			army_experience = 25
			navy_experience = 25
			air_experience = 25
		}
	}
}

#Floods
country_event = {
	id = germany.4
	title = germany.4.t
	desc = germany.4.d
	picture = GFX_event_germany_floods
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.4 immediate"
			add_stability = -0.05
			set_country_flag = GER_major_floods_flag
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_cdu_popularity_var_temp
				value = -0.03
			}
			GER_add_cdu = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_greens_popularity_var_temp
				value = 0.02
			}
			GER_add_greens = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_afd_popularity_var_temp
				value = 0.02
			}
			GER_add_afd = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_spd_popularity_var_temp
				value = 0.02
			}
			GER_add_spd = yes
			news_event = {
				id = germany.5
				hours = 6
			}
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 42
						state = 888
						state = 51
					}
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = GER_flooded
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.4.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_cdu_popularity_var_temp
				value = -0.03
			}
			GER_add_cdu = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_greens_popularity_var_temp
				value = 0.02
			}
			GER_add_greens = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_afd_popularity_var_temp
				value = 0.02
			}
			GER_add_afd = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_spd_popularity_var_temp
				value = 0.02
			}
			GER_add_spd = yes
			news_event = {
				id = germany.5
				hours = 6
			}
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 42
						state = 888
						state = 51
					}
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = GER_flooded
				}
				damage_building = {
					type = infrastructure
					damage = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Establishment of the DDR
country_event = {
	id = germany.6
	title = germany.6.t
	desc = germany.6.d
	picture = GFX_event_DDR_reunification
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.6 immediate"
			news_event = {
				id = germany.7
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_communist_tree_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_day_x_tree_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_nafo_tree_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_post_nato_war_tree_flag
			#load_focus_tree = GER_communist
			focus_unlock = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.6.a
		set_cosmetic_tag = GER_DDR_communist
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = -0.1
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communist
			elections_allowed = no
			#last_election = "[GetDateText]"
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_popularities = {
				communist = 55
				libertarian_socialist = 25
				social_democrat = 10
				totalitarian_socialist = 10
			}
		}
	}
}

#Day X
country_event = {
	id = germany.8
	title = germany.8.t
	desc = germany.8.d
	picture = GFX_Bundeswehr_Acting
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.8 immediate"
			set_cosmetic_tag = GER_day_x
			add_stability = -0.15
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascist
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			news_event = {
				id = news.187
				hours = 6
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascist
				elections_allowed = no
				#last_election = "[GetDateText]"
				election_frequency = 48
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_destroy_far_right_in_army_flag
				}
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = GER_radelsfuhrer
				ideology = national_spartanism
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_day_x_startocratic_nationalism_flag
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.8.a
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			long_name = GER_outlawed_long
			name = GER_outlawed_short
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			long_name = GER_outlawed_long
			name = GER_outlawed_short
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			long_name = GER_outlawed_long
			name = GER_outlawed_short
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = conservative
			long_name = GER_outlawed_long
			name = GER_outlawed_short
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = libertarian_socialist
			long_name = GER_outlawed_long
			name = GER_outlawed_short
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = communist
			long_name = GER_outlawed_long
			name = GER_outlawed_short
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalitarian_socialist
			long_name = GER_outlawed_long
			name = GER_outlawed_short
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_war_support = -0.1
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascist
				elections_allowed = no
				#last_election = "[GetDateText]"
				election_frequency = 48
			}
		}
		focus_unlock = yes
	}
}

	}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.11 immediate"
			focus_unlock = yes
			add_ideas = low_covid_cases
			set_country_flag = GER_COVID_ongoing
			activate_mission = GER_coronavirus_timer

				id = germany.33
				days = 175
			}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 64

						state = 52
						state = 51
					}

					modifier = USA_coronavirus_state
				}
			}
		}
	}

		effect_tooltip = {
			add_ideas = low_covid_cases

# Ascension of the Supreme Chancellor
country_event = {
	id = germany.12
	title = germany.12.t
	desc = germany.12.d
	picture = GFX_Supreme_Chancellor
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		always = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.12.a
		ai_chance = {
		    factor = 1
		    modifier = {
		        factor = 0
		        OR = {
		            has_game_rule = {
		                rule = The_GER_Radelsfuhrer_Mask
		                option = The_GER_Radelsfuhrer_Mask_2
		            }
		        }
		    }
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_country_leader_trait = trait_supreme_chancellor
		create_corps_commander = {
			name = "Rädelsführer"
			picture = "Rädelsführer.dds"
			traits = {
				war_hero
				trait_reckless
			}
			skill = 3
			attack_skill = 2
			defense_skill = 1
			planning_skill = 3
			logistics_skill = 4
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.12.b
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		ai_chance = {
		    factor = 1
		    modifier = {
		        factor = 0
		        OR = {
		            has_game_rule = {
		                rule = The_GER_Radelsfuhrer_Mask
		                option = The_GER_Radelsfuhrer_Mask_1
		            }
		        }
		    }
		}
		set_portraits = {
			character = GER_radelsfuhrer
			civilian = {
				large = "GFX_portrait_GER_rädelsführer_unmasked"
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_radelsfuhrer_unmasked_flag
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_country_leader_trait = trait_supreme_chancellor
		create_corps_commander = {
			name = "Rädelsführer"
			picture = "GFX_portrait_GER_rädelsführer_unmasked"
			traits = {
				war_hero
				trait_reckless
			}
			skill = 3
			attack_skill = 2
			defense_skill = 1
			planning_skill = 3
			logistics_skill = 4
		}
	}
}

# Formation of the European Internationale
country_event = {
	id = germany.13
	title = germany.13.t
	desc = germany.13.d
	picture = GFX_Supreme_Chancellor
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.13 immediate"
			hidden_effect = {
				GER = {
					create_faction = DDR_European_Internationale
					remove_faction_goal = faction_goal_the_atomic_race
					add_faction_goal = faction_goal_placeholder_long_term
					remove_faction_goal = faction_goal_a_military_base
					add_faction_goal = faction_goal_placeholder_medium_term
					add_faction_goal = faction_goal_placeholder_short_term
					add_to_faction = GER
				}
				news_event = {
					id = news.253
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.13.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = {
				create_faction = DDR_European_Internationale
				add_to_faction = GER
			}
		}
	}
}

#Ich Hatte Eine Kammeraden \\ German Loss
country_event = {
	id = germany.19
	title = germany.19.t
	desc = germany.19.d
	picture = GFX_German_Funeral
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.19 immediate"
			end_coalition = yes
			decrease_academic = yes
			decrease_poverty = yes
			decrease_poverty = yes
			decrease_farming = yes
			decrease_military = yes
			decrease_society = yes
			decrease_society = yes
			decrease_industry = yes
			add_war_support = -0.25
			GER_disable_cdu = yes
			GER_disable_spd = yes
			GER_disable_fdp = yes
			GER_disable_greens = yes
			GER_disable_afd = yes
			GER_disable_die_linke = yes
			GER_depression_recovery_effect = yes
			remove_ideas = {
				GER_anti_consumerism
				GER_green_new_deal
				GER_spd_welfare
				GER_spd_welfare1
				GER_spd_welfare2
				GER_spd_welfare3
				GER_invisible_hand
				GER_invisible_hand1
				GER_invisible_hand2
				GER_invisible_hand3
				GER_digitalization
				GER_nwp
				GER_oil_crash1
				GER_oil_crash2
				GER_oil_crash3
				GER_oil_crash4
				GER_oil_crash5
			}
			remove_power_balance = {
				id = GER_trust_bop
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = {
				modifier = GER_bundestag_dynamic
			}
			add_ideas = lower_conscription
			add_ideas = civilian_mobilization
			country_event = {
				id = germany.101
				days = 199
			}
			#log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.19 immediate 1"
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = SOV_cprf_won
				}
				country_event = {
					id = germany.75
					days = 14
				}
				clr_country_flag = GER_communist_tree_flag
				set_country_flag = GER_day_x_tree_flag
				clr_country_flag = GER_nafo_tree_flag
				clr_country_flag = GER_post_nato_war_tree_flag
				load_focus_tree = GER_day_x
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = SOV_ldpr_won
				}
				country_event = {
					id = germany.74
					days = 14
				}
				set_country_flag = GER_communist_tree_flag
				clr_country_flag = GER_day_x_tree_flag
				clr_country_flag = GER_nafo_tree_flag
				clr_country_flag = GER_post_nato_war_tree_flag
				load_focus_tree = GER_communist
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
				UKR = {
					remove_state_core = 93
					remove_state_core = 91
					remove_state_core = 199
					remove_state_core = 80
					remove_state_core = 89
					remove_state_core = 73
				}
				UFA = {
					add_state_core = 93
					add_state_core = 91
					add_state_core = 199
					add_state_core = 80
					add_state_core = 89
					add_state_core = 73
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = SOV_medvedev_won
				}
				country_event = {
					id = germany.75
					days = 14
				}
				country_event = {
					id = germany.184
					days = 21
				}
				clr_country_flag = GER_communist_tree_flag
				clr_country_flag = GER_day_x_tree_flag
				set_country_flag = GER_nafo_tree_flag
				clr_country_flag = GER_post_nato_war_tree_flag
				load_focus_tree = GER_NAFO_tree_initial				#TODO: Coder, kill this guy
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
			#log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.19 immediate 2"
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.19.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_coalition_collapse_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_society_level_decrease_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_military_level_decrease_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_industry_level_decrease_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_academy_level_decrease_tt
			custom_effect_tooltip = generic_poverty_level_increased_tt
			add_war_support = -0.25
			add_ideas = lower_conscription
			add_ideas = civilian_mobilization
		}
	}
}

#2021 Elections
country_event = {
	id = germany.57
	title = germany.57.t
	desc = germany.57.desc
	picture = GFX_GER_elections
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		date > 2021.1.1
		date < 2022.1.1
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = GER_election_season_flag
			end_coalition = yes
			country_event = {
				id = germany.244
				days = 3
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.57 immediate"
			clr_country_flag = GER_die_linke_won_2021_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_greens_won_2021_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_spd_won_2021_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_fdp_won_2021_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_cdu_won_2021_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_afd_won_2021_flag
			GER_who_won_elections = yes
			remove_ideas = GER_merkelreich_idea
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_die_linke_won_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GER_new_government_flag
					}
					set_power_balance = {
						id = GER_trust_bop
						left_side = GER_bad_side
						right_side = GER_good_side
						set_value = 0
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = libertarian_socialist
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				add_stability = -0.25
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = GER_support_die_linke_var_temp
					value = 0.05
				}
				GER_add_support_die_linke = yes
				add_ideas = GER_bodo_ramelow_hog
				clr_country_flag = GER_anti_extremism_agenda_flag
				set_country_flag = GER_linke_won_2021_chancellor_check_flag
				set_country_flag = GER_die_linke_won_2021_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_greens_won_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GER_new_government_flag
					}
					set_power_balance = {
						id = GER_trust_bop
						left_side = GER_bad_side
						right_side = GER_good_side
						set_value = 0
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = social_liberal
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				add_stability = -0.1
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = GER_support_greens_var_temp
					value = 0.05
				}
				GER_add_support_greens = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = GER_habeck_flag }
					add_ideas = GER_Habeck
				}
				else = {
					add_ideas = GER_Baerbock_hog
				}
				set_country_flag = GER_greens_won_2021_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_spd_won_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GER_new_government_flag
					}
					set_power_balance = {
						id = GER_trust_bop
						left_side = GER_bad_side
						right_side = GER_good_side
						set_value = 0
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = social_democrat
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				add_stability = -0.05
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = GER_support_spd_var_temp
					value = 0.05
				}
				GER_add_support_spd = yes
				add_ideas = GER_Scholz
				set_country_flag = GER_spd_won_2021_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_fdp_won_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {

					}

		}
	}

		name = germany.58.a
		remove_mission = GER_extreme_left_action
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = GER_greens_popularity_var_temp
			value = 0.03
		}
		GER_add_greens = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = GER_die_linke_popularity_var_temp
			value = 0.03
		}
		GER_add_die_linke = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = GER_afd_popularity_var_temp
			value = -0.03
		}
		GER_add_afd = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.58.b
		remove_mission = GER_extreme_right_action
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = GER_afd_popularity_var_temp
			value = 0.03
		}
		GER_add_afd = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = GER_die_linke_popularity_var_temp
			value = -0.03
		}
		GER_add_die_linke = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.58.c
		add_political_power = 150
		add_stability = -0.1
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = GER_cdu_popularity_var_temp
			value = 0.05
		}
		GER_add_cdu = yes

			var = GER_spd_popularity_var_temp
			value = 0.05
		}
		GER_add_spd = yes
		remove_mission = GER_extreme_right_action
		remove_mission = GER_extreme_left_action
	}
}

#German Stock Market Crash
country_event = {
	id = germany.69
	title = germany.69.t
	desc = germany.69.d
	picture = GFX_Bundestag
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.69 immediate"
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_ruling_popularity_var_temp
				value = -0.03
			}
			GER_add_ruling_party = yes
			set_country_flag = GER_depression_ongoing_flag
			add_to_variable = {
				var = GER_economy_min_export_dynamic_var
				value = -0.2
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = GER_economy_industrial_capacity_dockyard_dynamic_var
				value = -0.4
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = GER_economy_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor_dynamic_var
				value = -0.2
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = GER_economy_consumer_goods_factor_dynamic_var
				value = 0.4
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = GER_economy_poverty_development_monthly_dynamic_var
				value = -0.04
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_european_green_deal
				}
				set_variable = {
					var = GER_budget_sustainment_var
					value = 0
				}
				activate_mission = GER_budget_sustainment_mission
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.69.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_ruling_popularity_var_temp
				value = -0.03
			}
			GER_add_ruling_party = yes
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_peoples_economy_dummy_idea
				add_idea = GER_economic_devastation_idea
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_european_green_deal
				}
				activate_mission = GER_budget_sustainment_mission
			}
		}
		
	}
}

#Riots Across Germany
country_event = {
	id = germany.115
	title = germany.115.t
	desc = germany.115.d
	picture = GFX_Generic_Riot
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.115 immediate"
			country_event = {
				id = germany.115
				days = 21
			}
			add_stability = -0.03
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascist
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					popularity = 0.01
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = libertarian_socialist
					popularity = 0.01
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 0.01
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communist
					popularity = 0.03
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascist
					popularity = 0.03
				}
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = GER_end_riots
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.115.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.03
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascist
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					popularity = 0.02
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = libertarian_socialist
					popularity = 0.01
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_democrat
					popularity = 0.02
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communist
					popularity = 0.03
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascist

#Germany Demands our Subjegation
country_event = {
	id = germany.143
	title = germany.143.t
	desc = germany.143.d
	picture = GFX_Operation_Michael
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.143 immediate"
		}
	}
	option = {
		#accept
		name = germany.143.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SWE
			}
			country_event = {
				id = germany.145
			}
			GER = {
				add_to_faction = SWE
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = NOR
			}
			country_event = {
				id = germany.148
			}
			GER = {
				add_to_faction = NOR
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#deny
		name = germany.143.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SWE
			}
			country_event = {
				id = germany.146
				days = 35
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = germany.144
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = NOR
			}
			country_event = {
				id = germany.149
				days = 35
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = germany.147
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				factor = 10
				tag = PRS

			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				tag = PRP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				tag = GRK
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				tag = UK2
			}
		}
		GER_join_csw = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = BOL
					original_tag = COL
				}

				ruling_party = libertarian_socialist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = libertarian_socialist
				popularity = 0.2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					original_tag = PRU
					original_tag = ANG
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communist
				popularity = 0.2
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = -0.2
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = libertarian_socialist
				popularity = -0.2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			base = 3

		}

#Stasi Crackdown
country_event = {
	id = germany.191
	title = germany.191.t
	desc = germany.191.d
	picture = GFX_Stasi
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.191 immediate"
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.191.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = GER_new_stasi_idea
			add_idea = GER_new_stasi_2_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_anti_communist_underground_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_anti_communist_underground_2
				add_idea = GER_anti_communist_underground_1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_anti_communist_underground_1
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_anti_communist_underground_1
				add_idea = GER_anti_communist_underground
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = GER_anti_communist_underground
			}
			remove_ideas = GER_anti_communist_underground
		}
	}
}

#Establishment of Walled City
country_event = {
	id = germany.204
	title = germany.204.t
	desc = germany.204.d
	picture = GFX_Walled_City
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell1
			has_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell2
			has_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell3
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.204 immediate"
			country_event = {
				id = germany.204
				days = 720
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell1
						has_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell2
						has_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell3
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell1
				}
				set_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell2
				}
				set_country_flag = GER_urbanite_hell3
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = {
								modifier = GER_lined_city
							}
						}
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = GER_lined_city
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.204.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = {
								modifier = GER_lined_city
							}
						}
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = GER_lined_city
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			var = GER_afd_popularity_var_temp
			value = -0.03
		}
		GER_add_afd = yes
	}
	option = {
		#Max Otte Will Help Save Germany!
		name = germany.208.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GER_i_want_to_be_chuddy
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = GER_i_want_to_be_cdu
						has_completed_focus = GER_reconcile_the_parties
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = GER_afd_popularity_var_temp
			value = 0.03
		}
		GER_add_afd = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_reconcile_the_parties
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_cdu_popularity_var_temp
				value = 0.03
			}
			GER_add_cdu = yes
		}
	}
}

#2022 Presidential Election
country_event = {
	id = germany.209
	title = germany.209.t
	desc = germany.209.d
	picture = GFX_GER_bundestag_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = germany.400
				days = 1825
			}
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.209 immediate"
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_trabert_popularity_var_temp
				value = GER_die_linke_popularity_var
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_otte_popularity_var_temp
				value = GER_afd_popularity_var
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_steinmeir_popularity_var_temp
				value = GER_greens_popularity_var
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_steinmeir_popularity_var_temp
				value = GER_spd_popularity_var
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				var = GER_steinmeir_popularity_var_temp
				value = GER_fdp_popularity_var
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_reconcile_the_parties
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					var = GER_otte_popularity_var_temp
					value = GER_cdu_popularity_var
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					var = GER_steinmeir_popularity_var_temp
					value = GER_cdu_popularity_var
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							check_variable = {
								GER_steinmeir_popularity_var_temp < GER_otte_popularity_var_temp
							}
							check_variable = {
								GER_steinmeir_popularity_var_temp < GER_trabert_popularity_var_temp
							}
						}
					}
					add_political_power = 50
					set_country_flag = GER_steinmeir_won_flag
				}
				10 = {
					modifier = {
						factor = 0
						OR = {
							check_variable = {
								GER_otte_popularity_var_temp < GER_steinmeir_popularity_var_temp
							}
							check_variable = {
								GER_otte_popularity_var_temp < GER_trabert_popularity_var_temp
							}
						}
					}
					GER_frankwalter_steinmeir = {
						GER_remove_president = yes
					}
					GER_max_otte_char = {
						GER_add_president = yes
					}
					add_stability = 0.05
					set_country_flag = GER_otte_won_flag
				}
				#10 = {
				#	modifier = {
				#		factor = 0
				#		OR = {
				#			check_variable = {
				#				GER_trabert_popularity_var_temp < GER_otte_popularity_var_temp
				#			}
				#			check_variable = {
				#				GER_trabert_popularity_var_temp < GER_steinmeir_popularity_var_temp
				#			}
				#		}
				#	}
				#	GER_frankwalter_steinmeir = {
				#		GER_remove_president = yes
				#	}
				#	GER_gerhard_trabert_char = {
				#		GER_add_president = yes
				#	}
				#	add_stability = -0.05
				#	set_country_flag = GER_trabert_won_flag
				#}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		#Frank-Walter Steinmeier
		name = germany.209.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GER_steinmeir_won_flag
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		clr_country_flag = GER_steinmeir_won_flag
	}
	option = {
		#Max Otte
		name = germany.209.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GER_otte_won_flag
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		clr_country_flag = GER_otte_won_flag
	}
	option = {
		#Gerhard Trabert
		name = germany.209.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GER_trabert_won_flag
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_stability = -0.05
		}
		clr_country_flag = GER_trabert_won_flag
	}

#Corporate Coup
country_event = {
	id = germany.221
	title = germany.221.t
	desc = germany.221.d
	picture = GFX_Mona_Lisa
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.221 immediate"
			change_government_type_corporate_council = yes
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = GER_european_commission_char
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = corporatocracy
					desc = GER_EUROCOMMISSION_DESC
					expire = "1.1.1.1"
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
				election_frequency = 48
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.25
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				retire_character = GER_max_otte_char
				retire_character = GER_bernd_baumann
			}
			add_ideas = GER_Busch
			add_ideas = GER_Schwaub
			add_ideas = GER_Potsch
			add_ideas = GER_Bate
			add_ideas = GER_Eichelmann
			set_country_flag = GER_corporate_coup_flag
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = GER_volt_europa_corp_long
				name = GER_volt_europa_corp
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.221.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			change_government_type_corporate_council = yes
			add_stability = -0.1

		}

		}

			coalition_partner_var_temp = token:social_democrat
		}
		add_to_coalition = yes

			var = GER_support_spd_var_temp

			value = 0.05
		}
		GER_add_support_fdp = yes
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_timed_idea = {

#2025+ Elections
country_event = {
	id = germany.250
	title = germany.250.t
	desc = germany.250.desc
	picture = GFX_GER_elections
	fire_only_once = no
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		date > 2025.1.1
		#date < 2026.1.1
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.250 immediate"
			clr_country_flag = GER_election_season_flag
			end_coalition = yes
			country_event = {
				id = germany.244
				days = 3
			}
			clr_country_flag = GER_die_linke_won_2021_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_greens_won_2021_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_spd_won_2021_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_fdp_won_2021_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_cdu_won_2021_flag
			clr_country_flag = GER_afd_won_2021_flag
			GER_who_won_elections = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_die_linke_won_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GER_new_government_flag
					}
					set_power_balance = {
						id = GER_trust_bop
						left_side = GER_bad_side
						right_side = GER_good_side
						set_value = 0
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = libertarian_socialist
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = GER_linke_won_2021_chancellor_check_flag }
					add_ideas = GER_bodo_ramelow_hog
				}
				else = {
					add_ideas = GER_heidi_reichinnek_hog
				}
				clr_country_flag = GER_anti_extremism_agenda_flag
				set_country_flag = GER_die_linke_won_2021_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_greens_won_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GER_new_government_flag
					}
					set_power_balance = {
						id = GER_trust_bop
						left_side = GER_bad_side
						right_side = GER_good_side
						set_value = 0
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = social_liberal
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = GER_habeck_flag }
					add_ideas = GER_Habeck
				}
				else = {
					add_ideas = GER_Baerbock_hog
				}
				set_country_flag = GER_greens_won_2021_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_spd_won_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GER_new_government_flag
					}
					set_power_balance = {
						id = GER_trust_bop
						left_side = GER_bad_side
						right_side = GER_good_side
						set_value = 0
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = social_democrat
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				add_ideas = GER_Scholz
				set_country_flag = GER_spd_won_2021_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_fdp_won_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GER_new_government_flag
					}
					set_power_balance = {
						id = GER_trust_bop
						left_side = GER_bad_side
						right_side = GER_good_side
						set_value = 0
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = market_liberal
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				add_ideas = GER_christian_lindner_hog
				set_country_flag = GER_fdp_won_2021_flag
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_cdu_won_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GER_new_government_flag
					}
					set_power_balance = {
						id = GER_trust_bop
						left_side = GER_bad_side
						right_side = GER_good_side
						set_value = 0
					}
					set_politics = {

					}
				}

				}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				OR = {
					has_government = conservative
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = income_var_temp
			value = 100
		}
		add_income_with_inflation = yes
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = SOV_fanaticism_var_temp
			value = -0.05
		}
		SOV_add_fanaticism = yes
		add_ideas = GER_renewed_russian_german_trade_deal
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = germany.262
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.260.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_government = national_socialist
					has_government = totalitarian_socialist
				}
			}
		}
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = -150
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = germany.261
			}
		}
	}
}

				elections_allowed = no

				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = military_junta
					expire = "1.1.1.1"
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = FAF_Vichy_France
		}
	}
	option = { #French led
		name = germany.994.b
		if = {
			limit = {

				}	
			}

					ruling_party = national_socialist
					elections_allowed = no

				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = FAF_Jeremy_Mourain_char

						ideology = neonazism
						expire = "1.1.1.1"
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = FAF_Vichy_France_franz
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = GER_klaus_armstroff_char
					ruling_only = yes
				}	
			}
			FAF = {

					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = FAF_Frederic_Chatillon_char

					}

						}
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = FAF_Vichy_France_radelsfuhrer
			}
		}
		else_if = {

#Spartanist Takeover - Michael Koth

	id = germany.289
	title = germany.289.t
	desc = germany.289.d
	picture = GFX_GER_koth_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalitarian_socialist
				elections_allowed = no
				last_election = "1918.11.11"
				election_frequency = 48
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = GER_michael_koth_char
				picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/GER_michael_koth.png"
				expire = "1.1.1.1"
				ideology = left_wing_junta
				traits = {
					hog_old_guard
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = totalitarian_socialist
				popularity = 0.2
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascist
				popularity = 0.07
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_spartanist_flag
			focus_unlock = yes
			country_event = {
				id = germany.301
				days = 7
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascist
				long_name = PRC_suspended_party_long
				name = PRC_suspended_party
			}	
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_socialist
				long_name = PRC_suspended_party_long
				name = PRC_suspended_party
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var_temp = token:libertarian_socialist }
			remove_from_coalition = yes
			news_event = {
				id = news.597
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.289.a
		focus_unlock = yes
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = GER_spartanist_cat
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = totalitarian_socialist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}

				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			FPR = {
				create_faction = FPR_European_Internationale
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_faction_goal = faction_goal_the_atomic_race
					add_faction_goal = faction_goal_placeholder_long_term
					remove_faction_goal = faction_goal_a_military_base
					add_faction_goal = faction_goal_placeholder_medium_term
					add_faction_goal = faction_goal_placeholder_short_term
				}
				add_to_faction = RSR
				add_to_faction = PRP
				add_to_faction = ITA
				add_to_faction = UK2
				add_to_faction = GRK
				add_to_faction = LUX
			}
			GER = {
				create_faction = DDR_European_Internationale
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_faction_goal = faction_goal_the_atomic_race
					add_faction_goal = faction_goal_placeholder_long_term
					remove_faction_goal = faction_goal_a_military_base
					add_faction_goal = faction_goal_placeholder_medium_term
					add_faction_goal = faction_goal_placeholder_short_term
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.296.a
		
	}

			remove_from_coalition = yes

					}

country_event = {
	id = germany.999
	title = germany.999.t
	desc = germany.999.d
	picture = GFX_event_GER_pump_eet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event germany.999 immediate"
		}
	}
	trigger = {
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.999.a
		if = {
			limit = { is_debug = yes }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_he_bought_flag }
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = income_var_temp
					value = -10
				}
				add_income_with_inflation = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_he_bought
				set_country_flag = GER_he_bought_flag
				hidden_effect = {
					every_possible_country = {
						remove_ideas = GER_great_economic_boom_idea
					}
					news_event = news.417 
					add_GDP = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_he_bought_flag
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					var = income_var_temp
					value = 1
				}
				add_income_with_inflation = yes
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_he_sold
				clr_country_flag = GER_he_bought_flag
				hidden_effect = {
					every_possible_country = {
						remove_ideas = {
							generic_world_wide_financial_crisis_1
							generic_world_wide_financial_crisis_2
							generic_world_wide_financial_crisis_3
						}
						add_ideas = GER_great_economic_boom_idea
					}
					add_GDP = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#International Aid - Brownintern
country_event = {
	id = germany.1002
	title = germany.1002.t
	desc = germany.1002.d
	picture = GFX_Bundeswehr_Acting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
	}
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.1002.a
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = volunteers_var
			value = GER.max_manpower_k
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			volunteers_var = GER.has_war_support
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			volunteers_var = GER.party_popularity@ruling_party
		}
		divide_temp_variable = {
			volunteers_var = 40
		}
		add_manpower = volunteers_var
		set_temp_variable = {
			rifles_var = random
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			artillery_var = random
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			btr_var = random
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			bmp_var = random
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			fuel_var = random
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			rifles_var = 700
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			fuel_var = 700
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			artillery_var = 70
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			btr_var = 70
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			bmp_var = 70
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = rifles_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = spaa_equipment
			amount = artillery_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = mechanized_equipment
			amount = btr_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = light_mechanized_equipment
			amount = bmp_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				fuel_ratio > 0.5
			}
			add_fuel = fuel_var
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = germany.1003
	title = germany.1003.t
	desc = germany.1003.d
	picture = GFX_Bundeswehr_Acting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
	}
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.1003.a
		set_temp_variable = {
			var = volunteers_var
			value = GER.max_manpower_k
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			volunteers_var = GER.has_war_support
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			volunteers_var = GER.party_popularity@ruling_party
		}
		divide_temp_variable = {
			volunteers_var = 40
		}
		add_manpower = volunteers_var
		set_temp_variable = {
			rifles_var = random
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			artillery_var = random
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			btr_var = random
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			bmp_var = random
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			fuel_var = random
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			rifles_var = 700
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			fuel_var = 700
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			artillery_var = 70
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			btr_var = 70
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			bmp_var = 70
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = rifles_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = spaa_equipment
			amount = artillery_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = mechanized_equipment
			amount = btr_var
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = light_mechanized_equipment
			amount = bmp_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				fuel_ratio > 0.5
			}
			add_fuel = fuel_var
		}
	}
}

#Day X Ending
country_event = {
	id = germany.1111
	title = germany.1111.t
	desc = germany.1111.d
	picture = GFX_GER_endspiel
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.1111.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_tfr_germany_ending_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = novo_event_tt
	}
}

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.3333.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_tfr_germany_ending_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = novo_event_tt
	}

country_event = {
	id = germany.9998
	title = germany.9998.t
	desc = germany.9998.d
	picture = GFX_GER_endspiel
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = GER_formalize_the_european_union
		country_exists = KBK
		country_exists = BYA
		country_exists = SHL
		NOT = {
			country_exists = UKR
		}
	}
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = germany.9998.a
		KBK = {
			get_current_government_type = yes
			GER = {
				puppet = KBK
			}
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
		}
		BYA = {
			get_current_government_type = yes
			GER = {
				puppet = BYA
			}
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
		}
		SHL = {
			get_current_government_type = yes
			GER = {
				puppet = SHL
			}
			restore_previous_government_type = yes
		}
	}
}

#Russia - Who to support in Saudi CW

	desc = proxy.1.d
	picture = GFX_GER_endspiel
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = proxy.1.a
		set_country_flag = SOV_support_saudi_gov_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = proxy.1.b
		set_country_flag = SOV_support_saudi_hezbollah_flag
	}
}
